	focus = {
		id = UKR_state_arsenals
		icon = GFX_goal_munitions_factories
		cost = 5

		relative_position_id = UKR_the_army_and_the_state
		x = -3
		y = 1

		prerequisite = { focus = UKR_the_army_and_the_state }

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = UKR_revolt_over
					has_completed_focus = UKR_the_young_hetman
				}
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus UKR_state_arsenals"
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = UKR_state_arsenals
				bonus = 1
				uses = 1
				category = infantry_weapons
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_state_arsenals_tt
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { UKR_industrial_score < 25 } }
				set_temp_variable = { UKR_factory_bonus = 1 }
				add_political_power = 60
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { UKR_industrial_score < 50 } }
				set_temp_variable = { UKR_factory_bonus = 2 }
				add_political_power = 45
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { UKR_industrial_score < 75 } }
				set_temp_variable = { UKR_factory_bonus = 3 }
				add_political_power = 30
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { UKR_industrial_score < 100 } }
				set_temp_variable = { UKR_factory_bonus = 4 }
				add_political_power = 15
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { UKR_industrial_score > 99 } }
				set_temp_variable = { UKR_factory_bonus = 5 }
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				prioritize = { 202 }
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					free_building_slots = { building = arms_factory size > 0 include_locked = yes }
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = UKR_factory_bonus
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = UKR_factory_bonus
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = UKR_industrialisation_mission
					check_variable = { UKR_industrial_score < 25 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { UKR_influence_change = 7 }
				UKR_industrial_score = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = UKR_industrialisation_mission
					check_variable = { UKR_industrial_score < 50 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { UKR_influence_change = 5 }
				UKR_industrial_score = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = UKR_industrialisation_mission
					check_variable = { UKR_industrial_score < 75 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { UKR_influence_change = 3 }
				UKR_industrial_score = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = UKR_industrialisation_mission
					check_variable = { UKR_industrial_score < 100 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { UKR_influence_change = 1 }
				UKR_industrial_score = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = UKR_radicalism_increasing
					OR = {
						UKR_rrb_moderates_dominant = yes
						UKR_upsr_moderates_dominant = yes
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_inspectorate_radsoc_1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = UKR_radicalism_increasing
					OR = {
						UKR_rrb_radicals_dominant = yes
						UKR_upsr_radicals_dominant = yes
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_inspectorate_radsoc_2
				add_political_power = 50
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
	}

						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KR_cooperative_advocate_2 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						UKR_pavlo_khrystiuk = { has_trait = KR_veteran_of_revolutionary_struggle_sic }
					}
					remove_trait = {
						character = UKR_pavlo_khrystiuk
						slot = second_in_command
						trait = KR_veteran_of_revolutionary_struggle_sic
					}
					add_trait = {
						character = UKR_pavlo_khrystiuk
						slot = second_in_command
						trait = KR_veteran_of_revolutionary_struggle_sic_2
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KR_veteran_of_revolutionary_struggle_2 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY }
	}

	focus = {
		id = UKR_all_peoples_revolutionary_front
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_agriculture2

			hidden_effect = {
				remove_trait = {
					character = UKR_mykola_kovalevskyi
					slot = second_in_command
					trait = KR_agricultural_economist
				}
				add_trait = {
					character = UKR_mykola_kovalevskyi
					slot = second_in_command
					trait = KR_agricultural_economist_2
				}
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KR_agricultural_economist_2 }
			}
		}

	}

	focus = {
		id = UKR_revolutionary_tradition
		icon = GFX_goal_revolution_tools
